msg:The hotel is located opposite the Yangzhou Municipal Government, not far from the Slender West Lake. You can ride a shared electric car on the roadside to get there, and the taxi is just the starting price.
The security uncle at the door, the front desk staff, and the room service staff are all very good. After checking out, I waited for the car at the door and asked the license plate number to help us pay attention to the car on the road. It happened that the taxi we took drove away without paying attention, and the hotel staff helped us stop the driver~ Special thanks to Xiao Yu and Xiao Ni!
The room is not big, but the facilities are complete. The hair dryer is Dyson, and it is also equipped with various hair dryers, which is very convenient for hair drying. The toilet and shower are also separated, which is convenient for simultaneous use. It is particularly worth mentioning that when you get up at night, the light under the bedside table will automatically light up, and it is not dazzling, and then there is also a circle of light in the toilet, just without turning on the light. This detail is not available in the hotel where I live for more than 4,000 a night!
I didn't book the hotel's breakfast, because Yangzhou breakfast is very special. There is a Liqun Plaza within a 10-minute walk, and there is a Gonghechun there, which is a very affordable traditional Yangzhou breakfast. There is also a Yongxiang noodle house, and the Su-style mixed noodles are very delicious, highly recommended!
